**Candidate 46:** `T*c0*epsilon*exp(c1*epsilon) + T*c2*log(c3*epsilon + 1) + c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6 + c7*log(c8*epsilon + 1)`

Going through all candidates systematically, none of them contain both `T*log(epsilon+1)` and `epsilon^2` terms simultaneously (or the ability to generate them). The GT requires the product T*log(epsilon+1), and very few candidates have T multiplied by log. Candidate 46 has it but can't produce epsilon^2 + epsilon from exp.
